 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:12%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;1.01. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On May&#160;19, 2020, JDE Peet&#8217;s B.V. (renamed JDE Peet&#8217;s N.V. immediately prior to Settlement (as defined below), &#8220;JDE Peet&#8217;s&#8221;) announced its intention to launch an offering of its ordinary shares (&#8220;ordinary shares&#8221;) (the &#8220;offering&#8221;) and to apply for admission to listing and trading of all of its ordinary shares on Euronext Amsterdam, a regulated market operated by Euronext Amsterdam N.V. (the &#8220;admission&#8221;). On May&#160;26, 2020, JDE Peet&#8217;s published a prospectus in connection with the offering and the admission. On May&#160;29, 2020, JDE Peet&#8217;s announced the final pricing terms of the offering, and JDE Peet&#8217;s and the selling shareholders, including us, agreed to sell at a price of <span style="font-family:Euro Serif">&#8364;</span>31.50 per ordinary share a total of 71,428,571 ordinary shares, or 82,142,856 ordinary shares if an option granted to the stabilization manager (on behalf of the underwriters) to cover for over-allotments of ordinary shares in the offering (&#8220;over-allotment option&#8221;) is exercised in full. The ordinary shares were listed and first traded on May&#160;29, 2020 (the &#8220;First Trading Date&#8221;), and payment for, and delivery of, the ordinary shares sold in the offering took place on June&#160;2, 2020 (&#8220;Settlement&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Prior to Settlement, we exchanged our ownership interest in <span style="text-transform:uppercase">Jacobs Douwe Egberts</span> B.V. (&#8220;JDE&#8221;) for an equity interest in JDE Peet&#8217;s. We did not invest new capital in connection with the transaction. We exchanged our 26.4% interest in JDE for a 26.5% interest in JDE Peet&#8217;s. We sold 9,661,835 of our ordinary shares in JDE Peet&#8217;s to buyers in the offering for gross proceeds of <span style="font-family:Euro Serif">&#8364;</span>304,347,802.50. We have granted the stabilization manager (on behalf of the underwriters) an over-allotment option requiring us to sell up to another 1,449,275 of our ordinary shares in JDE Peet&#8217;s. Following Settlement, we will hold between 22.9% and 23.4% of JDE Peet&#8217;s depending upon the exercise of the over-allotment option. We have agreed not to sell or otherwise dispose of our remaining ordinary shares in JDE Peet&#8217;s for a period of 180 days following Settlement, subject to customary exceptions. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Investor Rights Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">In connection with the transaction, Mondelez Coffee HoldCo B.V., a subsidiary of Mondel&#275;z International, Inc., entered into an agreement that governs our rights and obligations as a shareholder in JDE Peet&#8217;s (the &#8220;Investor Rights Agreement&#8221;). The Investor Rights Agreement became effective on the First Trading Date. It provides that we have the right to designate for nomination two <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</span> directors to the JDE Peet&#8217;s board. If our equity interest declines to less than 8%, we have the right to designate for nomination only one <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</span> director to the JDE Peet&#8217;s board. If our interest declines to less than 5%, we do not have the right to designate for nomination a <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</span> director. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Investor Rights Agreement is qualified in its entirety by the complete terms and conditions of the Investor Rights Agreement, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.1 and is incorporated by reference herein. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:12%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;1.02. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Termination of a Material Definitive Agreement.<span style="font-style:Italic">&#32;</span></td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">JDE Shareholders&#8217; Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">In connection with the transaction, Mondelez Coffee HoldCo B.V. entered into a letter agreement amending and terminating the shareholders&#8217; agreement that it previously entered into with Delta Charger HoldCo B.V., JDE Minority Holdings B.V. and JDE in relation to JDE (the &#8220;JDE Shareholders&#8217; Agreement&#8221;). This letter agreement amends the JDE Shareholders&#8217; Agreement by removing from the definition of surviving provisions certain covenants relating to <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-competition</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-solicitation,</span> and terminates the JDE Shareholders&#8217; Agreement in accordance with its terms. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the letter agreement is qualified in its entirety by reference to the complete terms and conditions of the letter agreement, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.2 and is incorporated by reference herein. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:12%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;8.01. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Other Events.<span style="font-style:Italic">&#32;</span></td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On May&#160;29, 2020, we issued a press release relating to our sale of JDE Peet&#8217;s shares in the offering. The press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span> and is being filed in accordance with Rule 135(c) under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Except for clause 1, this clause 2, clause 12.1 and clause 14, which will be effective upon execution of this Agreement, this Agreement will be
conditional upon and only enter into effect on the occurrence of the First Trading Date and shall thereafter continue until terminated pursuant to clause 10. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>LARGE COMPANY REGIME </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The parties acknowledge and agree that (a)&nbsp;the Company will act as the holding company of the Company Group and will not apply the large
company regime (<I>structuurregime</I>) and (b)&nbsp;no Group Company will apply the large company regime (<I>structuurregime</I>) unless required to do so under Dutch law (in which case, the parties must agree the manner in which that regime is
implemented so as to ensure that their rights set out in this Agreement are preserved and not adversely impacted in any respect. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Except to the extent required to comply with applicable Law, and without prejudice to clause 8.4, the

obligations, or in the exercise or enforcement of any of its rights, under or pursuant to this Agreement shall constitute a breach of this clause 4. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>5.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>RELATED PARTY TRANSACTIONS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Parties acknowledge the importance of, and shall ensure that, Related Party Transactions (as defined in the
Related Party Transaction Policy), including transactions between the Company and its subsidiaries, on the one hand, and any Related Party (as defined in the Related Party Transactions Policy) on the other hand, shall be on arms&#146; length terms
and shall be dealt with in accordance with the applicable legal, accounting and disclosure framework. Accordingly, the Company shall on or prior to the point at which MDLZ first holds shares in the Company (the <B>Effective Date</B>) (which is
expected to be shortly before the Settlement Date) have adopted the related party transactions policy in the agreed form attached as Schedule 6 (the <B>Related Party Transactions Policy</B>). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Subject to clause 8.5, an amendment of the Related Party Transactions Policy requires the approval of the
Board<I>, </I>including the affirmative vote of at least one Independent Board Member. No amendment of the Related Party Transactions Policy shall be proposed that would contravene, or be contrary to, any provision of this Agreement.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Designation rights </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

the Shares, then the number of directors on the Board MDLZ shall be entitled to designate shall be reduced to one. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

relevant General Meeting, Acorn will vote in favour of the appointments under clause 6.1 and this clause 6.4. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Board

than any decision that has been authorized by the any of the Board&#146;s committees duly authorized to take such action); or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ix)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">the approval of a decision which may have a material implication for the reputation of the Company Group;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">provided, further, after MDLZ and its Affiliates own less than 5% of the Shares, the Board Authority Matters shall
automatically and without any further action be deleted in their entirety (it being noted that the board of the Company will continue to consider those matters required by the Rules and as would generally be considered by the board of a Dutch listed
company). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Shareholders shall exercise their voting rights in each General Meeting in respect of the appointment and
dismissal of members of the Board in such a way as to give effect to this clause 6. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Expiry of the designation right
</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If MDLZ and its Affiliates (taken together) at any time beneficially own less than 5% of the Shares then the
number of directors on the Board MDLZ shall be entitled to designate shall be reduced to zero. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If MDLZ&#146;s shareholding falls below a threshold set out in clause 6.2 or 6.8, it shall:
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(i)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">inform the chairman of the Board thereof in writing within five (5)&nbsp;Business Days thereafter; and
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">procure the prompt resignation of one or both of its designated Board members (as required).
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Board may resolve, when a position is vacant as a result of a resignation pursuant to clause 6.9, that
either (a)&nbsp;a new candidate will be nominated to fill the vacancy, or (b)&nbsp;the vacancy will not be filled and the total number of Board members will be decreased. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.11</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Any designation right that expires as referenced in clause 6.2 or clause 6.8 shall not revive, regardless of
any subsequent increase of the Shareholder&#146;s shareholding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.12</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company shall not include the suspension or dismissal of a Board member appointed upon designation by MDLZ
on the agenda for a General Meeting of the Company except (i)&nbsp;in case of gross negligence, wilful misconduct, breach of any applicable laws, an official public incrimination, convictions, sanctions by statutory or regulatory authorities
(including designated professional bodies), fraud or a serious suspicion of fraud, or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
seriously culpable acts (<I>ernstig verwijtbaar handelen</I>) that (x)&nbsp;is supported by evidence and (y)&nbsp;relates to the Company or might reasonably be expected to bring the Company into
disrepute or (ii)&nbsp;when this has explicitly been requested by shareholder(s) of the Company in accordance with Section&nbsp;2:114a of the Dutch Civil Code, provided that the Company shall not serve any notice on a Board Member appointed by the
Shareholder without consulting, in good faith, with the Shareholder that appointed such Board Member, taking into consideration, in good faith, any such arguments that the Shareholder may raise opposing such suspension or dismissal prior to taking
any decision on such matters. The period of consultation shall be determined by the Board, and shall not be less than 90 days and shall not exceed 180 days. Notwithstanding the above, Acorn will not, and will procure that none of its Affiliates
holding Shares will, make any request of the kind referred to in (ii)&nbsp;above or vote in favour of suspension or dismissal of any Board member nominated by MDLZ, except in the cases referred to in (i)&nbsp;above where the relevant behaviour is
specific to that Board member (rather than related to the Board or a Board committee generally). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Board Committees
</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

audit committee and (ii)&nbsp;a selection, appointment and remuneration committee. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company shall ensure that at all times: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">a.</TD>

independent within the meaning of the Dutch Corporate Governance Code; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

remuneration committee. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Company to the maximum extent allowed under the Rules. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">For so long as MDLZ may designate two members of the Board, to the extent allowed under the Rules, MDLZ shall
be entitled to designate the chair of the audit committee of the Company. If that is not allowed under the Rules, then MDLZ shall nominate a member of the Board who is independent under the Rules as chair of the Audit Committee, provided that if at
any time thereafter, MDLZ is allowed to designate the chairman under the Rules, then it shall be entitled to replace the then serving chairman with its designee. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Governance and Concert </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.17</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Subject to clause 6.7, Acorn and MDLZ may prior to a General Meeting from time to time choose to consult each
other and to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-ordinate</FONT> the exercise of the voting rights attaching to the Shares held by them (and their Affiliates) from time to time in such General Meeting, without being required to agree with each other
in each case on the way such voting rights are exercised. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.18</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each of Acorn and MDLZ acknowledges and agrees that the Dutch public offer rules as laid down in the Dutch
Financial Supervision Act (<I>Wet op het financieel toezicht</I>) (the <B>FSA</B>) will, as of the First Trading Date, be applicable to the Company and its shareholders. As Acorn and MDLZ will continue to have a combined Voting Interest of more than
30% on the First Trading Date and have made the agreements set out in clause 6.7, Acorn and MDLZ agree to be deemed to jointly have substantial control (<I>gezamenlijke</I> <I>overwegende zeggenschap</I>) over the Company within the meaning of the
FSA and agree to remain qualified as concert parties (<I>in overleg handelende personen</I>) (each a <B>Concert Party</B> and together, a <B>Concert</B>) from the First Trading Date. On this basis, Acorn and MDLZ as well as their ultimate
Controlling persons, benefit from the exemption from the Dutch mandatory offer requirement as laid down in article 5:71 sub 1(i) of the FSA. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.19</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each of Acorn and MDLZ furthermore acknowledges and agrees that if, after the First Trading Date, a Third Party
acquires Control over it and this Agreement is still in effect, such Third Party may be deemed to acquire indirect substantial control (<I>overwegende zeggenschap</I>) over the Company. If such a scenario where such Third Party does acquire indirect
substantial control (<I>overwegende zeggenschap</I>) over the Company, the exemption from the Dutch mandatory offer requirement laid down in article 5:71 sub 1(i) of the FSA that is available to Acorn and MDLZ as well as their ultimate Controlling
persons from the First Trading Date, shall not be available to such Third Party acquiring control. Therefore, the occurrence of a Change of Control in relation to Acorn or MDLZ that results in a Third Party acquiring indirect substantial control
(<I>overwegende zeggenschap</I>) over the Company will result in immediate and automatic termination of the Concert and clauses 6.17 to 6.22 and of clause 6.7, unless maintaining clause 6.7 does not create a requirement for Acorn or MDLZ jointly or
individually to make a public offer (<I>openbaar bod</I>) for any equity securities in the Company in accordance with the Dutch mandatory takeover rules (a &#147;<B>Mandatory Offer</B>&#148;). For the purposes of this clause 6.19, <B>Change of
Control</B> shall mean a Third Party obtaining an interest or position in Acorn or MDLZ (whether directly or indirectly) which allows this Third Party to exercise Control over how Acorn or MDLZ votes its Shares. Each of Acorn and MDLZ shall notify
the other promptly after the occurrence of a Change of Control in respect of itself. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.20</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each of Acorn and MDLZ also acknowledges and agrees that if during the term of this Agreement their combined
Voting Interest drops below 30% for whatever reason, they will no longer benefit from the exemption from the Dutch mandatory offer requirement as laid down in article 5:71 sub 1(i) of the FSA (even if this Agreement is still in force), including in
case Acorn and MDLZ&#146;s combined Voting Interest is subsequently increased above 30%. Therefore, Acorn and MDLZ&#146;s combined Voting Interest dropping below 30% will result in immediate and automatic termination of the Concert and clauses 6.17
to 6.22. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.21</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each of Acorn and MDLZ acknowledges and agrees that as a result of the Concert, they are required under section
5.3 of the FSA to notify their holdings in the Company on a combined and aggregated basis to the AFM. Against this background, each of Acorn and MDLZ will promptly inform the other after having entered into any transaction in securities in relation
to the Company, and each will provide the other with details that are reasonably required to jointly assess whether notification in accordance with section 5.3 of the FSA must be made that one or more of the applicable notification thresholds has
been reached or crossed. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.22</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If Acorn or MDLZ or any of their respective Affiliates (whether acting alone or as a part of a consortium)
makes a public offer for any equity securities in the Company (whether voluntarily or as a Mandatory Offer), announces its intention and/or the requirement to launch such an offer, or does anything (or omits to do anything) that creates a
requirement for Acorn or MDLZ jointly or individually to make a Mandatory Offer, this will result in the immediate and automatic termination of the Concert and clauses 6.17 to 6.22 of clause 6.7 (unless maintaining clause 6.7 does not create a
requirement for MDLZ jointly or individually to make Mandatory Offer) and of clause 8. For avoidance of doubt this clause 6.22 shall not prevent Acorn and MDLZ from effecting or cooperating with a Change of Control over itself.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>7.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>INFORMATION </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company shall provide to a Shareholder (a)&nbsp;within 60 days after the end of each fiscal year, the
consolidated financial results for the Company Group for such fiscal year (including a profit and loss account, balance sheet, cash flow and statement of other comprehensive income) plus reconciliation from IFRS to US&nbsp;GAAP to the extent
required to satisfy the public reporting requirements of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group; provided, that such reconciliation shall be performed at such Shareholder&#146;s sole cost (or the Shareholders&#146; joint cost if
they both need such reconciliation), (b) promptly upon availability, the annual accounts of each member of the Company Group (except where such accounts or audits are not legally required), (c) within 30 days after the end of each fiscal quarter,
interim unaudited consolidated condensed financial results of the Company Group (including a profit and loss account, balance sheet, cash flow and statement of other comprehensive income) plus reconciliation from IFRS to US&nbsp;GAAP to the extent
required to satisfy the public reporting requirements of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group; provided, that such reconciliation shall be performed at such Shareholder&#146;s sole cost (or the Shareholders&#146; joint cost if
they both need such reconciliation), and (d)&nbsp;within such time as it is requested, such other financial information or documents in the possession of the Company and any of its Subsidiaries as such Shareholder may reasonably request in writing
in connection with the preparation of the Shareholder Public Filings of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group. MDLZ and the Company may agree from time to time the approach to be taken by Mondel&#275;z International for reporting
Company financial information in its Shareholder Public Filings in order to ensure compliance with Mondel&#275;z International&#146;s reporting obligations and the Rules. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company and each Shareholder will coordinate the timing of their respective releases for as long as the
information relating to the Company as shown in the Shareholder Public Filings of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group is material to the Company share price, subject always to the reporting obligations of any member of that
Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company shall cooperate, and use its reasonable best efforts to cause the Auditor to cooperate, with a
Shareholder to the extent reasonably requested in writing by such Shareholder in the preparation of the Shareholder Public Filings of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group. The Company agrees to use its reasonable best efforts to
provide to such Shareholder all information that such Shareholder reasonably requests in writing in connection with any Shareholder Public Filings of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group that, in the reasonable judgment of such
Shareholder upon consultation with its legal counsel, is required to be disclosed or incorporated by reference therein under any Rules (including any stock exchange rules applicable to the relevant member(s) of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder
Group). The Company shall use its reasonable best efforts to provide such information to enable each Shareholder to prepare and release all Shareholder Public Filings of any member of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group on a timely basis. To
the extent required in such filing, the Company shall use its reasonable best efforts to cause the Auditor to consent to any reference to them as experts in any Shareholder Public Filings required under the Rules (including any stock exchange rules
applicable to the relevant member(s) of that Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group). The Company shall procure that the Auditor will provide an audit opinion to the Shareholder&#146;s external auditors (or those of any member of its Shareholder
Group) on the Company&#146;s financial statements for each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> period beginning on each 1&nbsp;October and ending on 30&nbsp;September in the following calendar year; provided, that such audit opinion
shall be prepared at such Shareholder&#146;s sole cost. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company will, within 25 days after the end of each fiscal quarter, make the Company&#146;s controller
available for a discussion with a Shareholder with regards to updates to the Company&#146;s business and financial results with respect to such fiscal quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Information will be provided to all members of the Board equally (including the Company directors representing
Shareholders), except to the extent prohibited under the Rules, and the Company directors representing Shareholders may share that information with the relevant Shareholder to the extent necessary to allow it to monitor and evaluate its
participation in the Company; provided, that such Shareholder shall enter into a customary confidentiality agreement with the Company. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>8.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>ARTICLES OF ASSOCIATION, BOARD RULES, KOREA PROTOCOL AND RELATED PARTY TRANSACTION POLICY
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Parties shall procure that the Articles of Association will, on or prior to the First Trading Date, be
amended into the agreed form, which is attached hereto as Schedule 3. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Parties agree that on or prior to the First Trading Date the Board will adopt (1)&nbsp;the Board Rules and
(2)&nbsp;the Korea Protocol in each case in the agreed form attached hereto as Schedule 4 and 5 respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">An amendment of the Articles of Association or the Board Rules can be made in accordance with the Rules and as
described in the relevant document. However, no amendment of the Articles of Association or the Board Rules shall be proposed by a Party that would contravene, or be contrary to, any provision of this Agreement. The Parties shall exercise their
rights in a manner consistent with this Clause 8.3. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Parties shall do all that is reasonably possible to achieve an amendment of the Articles of Association
and/or the Board Rules if and to the extent such documents contravene, or are contrary to, or inconsistent with, any provision of this Agreement, including, in the case of each Shareholder, exercising its voting or other shareholder rights and
powers to do so (and procuring that any of its relevant Affiliates do the same). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">For so long as MDLZ is entitled to designate at least one director to the Board, the Company shall not amend or
terminate the Related Party Transaction Policy or the Korea Protocol (the <B>Policies</B>) without MDLZ&#146;s prior written consent, such consent not to be unreasonably withheld in the case of an amendment required by the Rules; thereafter, the
Policies can be amended or terminated as permitted by the Rules. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>9.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>ORDERLY MARKET ARRANGEMENTS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Sell Down </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">At any time after the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Lock-up</FONT> Period, each Shareholder (and any
transferee pursuant to a transfer permitted under clause 13.1) is entitled to sell, transfer or otherwise dispose of any number of Shares, in the open market, through a private sale or otherwise (a <B>Sell Down</B>). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Subject to clause 9.2 and the remainder of this clause 9.2, so long as both Acorn and MDLZ have at least one
representative serving as a member of the Board, if a Shareholder has a <I>bona fide</I> intention to execute a Sell Down in accordance with clause 9.1 (the <B>Selling Shareholder</B>), the Selling Shareholder shall notify the other Shareholder (the
<B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder</B>) in writing of that intention (an <B>Intent to Sell Notice</B>) at least two Business Days&#146; in advance of that Sell Down. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Selling Shareholder gives a <I>bona fide</I> Intent to Sell Notice, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder
may not sell any Shares from receipt of that notice until the earlier of (a)&nbsp;the fifth Business Day following receipt of that notice and (b)&nbsp;the time at which the Selling Shareholder sells the Shares to which that notice relates. For this
purpose, the Selling Shareholder shall notify the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder promptly of the consummation of such sale. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Once the Selling Shareholder sells the Shares to which the notice relates, it may not serve another Intent to Sell Notice for five Business
Days after the date of that sale. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Selling Shareholder has not sold all the Shares to which notice relates within 10
Business Days following receipt by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder of a Intent to Sell Notice: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">a.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder shall be entitled to assume that the Sell
Down will not take place; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">b.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">the Selling Shareholder may not serve another Intent to Sell Notice for five Business Days after the expiry of
that 10 Business Day period. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder shall keep any notice
received under this clause 9.2 confidential. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Following receipt of an Intent to Sell Notice, the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder may notify the Selling Shareholder that it does not wish to receive any further information about the proposed Sell Down to which that notice relates. If the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder does so, the Selling Shareholder must not provide any such information to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder, other than to notify the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder of the consummation of a sale as required by this clause 9.2 or otherwise as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Selling</FONT> Shareholder requests. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Clause 9.2 shall not apply to the extent that a Shareholder (or relevant transferee) sells, transfers or
otherwise disposes of Shares: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">a.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">by way of acceptance of a public takeover offer, merger or similar business combination in respect of all of
the issued Shares; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">b.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">by way of acceptance of a partial public takeover offer in respect of part of the Shares as permitted by Dutch
law; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">c.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">to a Permitted Transferee (as defined in clause 13.1); </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">d.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">pursuant to a compromise or arrangement between the Company and its creditors or any class of them or between
the Company and its members or any class of them, in each case which is agreed to by the creditors or members of the Company; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">e.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">where required by law or competent governmental authority. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Clauses 9.1 to 9.2 confer rights and obligations on the Shareholders only. In particular, the Company will have
no rights or obligations arising out of these clauses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company will cooperate with the selling Shareholder(s) to optimise any Sell Down, including but not limited
to (a)&nbsp;providing reasonable access to information required for a due diligence and drafting of any required documentation, (b)&nbsp;providing assistance in obtaining regulatory, stock exchange and other approvals required for a Sell Down and
(c)&nbsp;being a party to an underwriting agreement containing customary provisions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each Party shall ensure that any Sell Down, including communication relating to a Sell Down, will be conducted
in compliance with applicable law, including the Market Abuse Regulation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company cannot be required to apply for a secondary listing of the Shares. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Costs and expenses </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">All fees and expenses in connection with a transfer of Shares by a Shareholder, including all fees and external
expenses incurred by the Company in connection with the preparation of such transfer (including but not limited to the preparation of a prospectus) and fees properly incurred by book runner(s) and their legal advisers (if any), will:
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">if the Company does not issue any Shares in conjunction with such transfer (nor transfer Shares held in its own
capital), be borne by the selling Shareholder(s) proportionate to the number of Shares issued or transferred by each of them; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">if the Company issues or transfers Shares in conjunction with such transfer, be shared <I>pro rata</I> by the
Company and the selling Shareholder(s), proportionate to the number of Shares issued or transferred by each of them, </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">in
either case, except for any fees and external expenses of the bookrunner appointed at the instruction of the Company, which will be borne by the Company to the extent such fees and external expenses are additionally incurred as a result of such
appointment. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

full force and effect unless amended in accordance with their terms), shall: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

from time to time) to acknowledge receipt of any notice receive by email within one Business Day of receipt. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>No Assignment </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">This Agreement is personal to the Parties and accordingly a Party may not assign, transfer or encumber
(<I>goederenrechtelijk onoverdraagbaar en niet te bezwaren</I>), in accordance with Section&nbsp;3:83 paragraph 2 of the Dutch Civil Code, grant any security interest over or create any trust in respect of, or purpose to assign, transfer, grant any
security interest over or create any trust in respect of any rights or obligations arising under this Agreement without the prior written consent of the other Parties, in respect of which each Party may decide in its own discretion, provided that
each Shareholder may freely assign or transfer its rights and obligations under this Agreement to a member of its Shareholder Group (each a <B>Permitted Transferee</B>), but only together with all or part of its Shares and provided such new holder
of Shares shall become a party to this Agreement by entering into a deed of adherence and that if such new holder ceases to be a member of the transferring Shareholder&#146;s Shareholder Group, it shall transfer the shares back to the transferring
Shareholder or to another member of the same Shareholder Group prior to such cessation. For purposes of calculation of the percentages under clauses 6.2, 6.5, 6.6, 6.8, 6.16, 6.18 and 6.20, the Shares held by any Permitted Transferee shall be deemed
to be held by the Shareholder that transferred its Shares to such Permitted Transferee. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Costs and expenses </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unless explicitly provided otherwise in this Agreement, the Parties shall each bear their own costs, charges
and expenses incurred in relation to this Agreement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>No rescission </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Each Party hereby waives, to the extent permitted by law, the right to partially or wholly rescind
(<I>ontbinden</I>) or partially or wholly nullify (<I>vernietigen</I>) or otherwise terminate this Agreement. The Parties hereby agree to exclude the applicability of Section&nbsp;6:230, paragraph 2 of the Dutch Civil Code. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Several and not joint liability </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Any provision of this Agreement which is expressed to bind more than one person shall bind them severally and
not jointly or jointly and severally, unless it is expressly provided otherwise. Breach of this Agreement by one Party shall not constitute a breach of this Agreement by another Party. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Severability </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If a provision of this Agreement is or becomes invalid or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding,</FONT>
the Parties shall remain bound by the remaining provisions. In that event, the Parties shall replace the invalid or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</FONT> provision by provisions that are valid and binding and that have, to the greatest
extent possible, a similar effect as the invalid or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</FONT> provision, given the contents and purpose of this Agreement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>No implied waiver </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Nothing shall be construed as a waiver under this Agreement unless a document to that effect has been signed by
the Parties or a notice to that effect has been given. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

the right to exercise or enforce such right in the future. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:5%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Entire agreement </B></P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">means the power of a person (or persons acting in concert) to secure that the affairs of another are conducted directly or indirectly in
accordance with the wishes of that person (or persons acting in concert) including by means of:</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) in the case of a company, being the beneficial owner of more than 50% of the issued share capital of or of the voting rights in that company, or having the
right to appoint or remove a majority of the directors or otherwise control the votes at board meetings of that company by virtue of any powers conferred by the articles of association, shareholders&#146; agreement or any other document regulating
the affairs of that company; or</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) in the case of a partnership, being the
beneficial owner of more than 50% of the capital of that partnership, or having the right to control the composition of or the votes of the majority of the management of that partnership by virtue of any powers conferred by the partnership agreement
or any other document regulating the affairs of that partnership,</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">and <B>Controlling
</B>and<B> Controlled</B> shall be construed accordingly. For these purposes, &#147;persons acting in concert&#148;, in relation to a person, are persons which actively <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-operate</FONT> pursuant to an agreement or
understanding (whether formal or informal) with a view to obtaining, maintaining or consolidating Control of that person</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In this Agreement, unless specified otherwise: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="6%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">(i) a <B>subsidiary</B> of an undertaking (<B>A</B>)&nbsp;is to any other undertaking, the business affairs of
which can be directed by A either directly or indirectly, alone or together with group entities, through the exercise or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exercise</FONT> of any voting power in any meeting of shareholders or in any meeting of
managing directors (<I>bestuur</I>) or supervisory directors (<I>raad van commissarissen</I>) (if any) or managers or otherwise, whether by agreement or otherwise; and (ii)&nbsp;a <B>parent</B> of an undertaking (<B>B</B>)&nbsp;is to any other
undertaking who can direct the business affairs of B either directly or indirectly, alone or together with group entities, through the exercise or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exercise</FONT> of any voting power in any meeting of
shareholders or in any meeting of managing directors (<I>bestuur</I>) or supervisory directors (<I>raad van commissarissen</I>) (if any) or managers or otherwise, whether by agreement or otherwise; (iii)&nbsp;a parent shall be treated as the parent
of undertakings in relation to which any of its subsidiaries are, or are to be treated, as parents, and references to subsidiaries shall be construed accordingly; and (iv)&nbsp;a <B>wholly owned</B> undertaking of another undertaking
(<B>C</B>)&nbsp;includes an undertaking that C would own 100% of the shares or voting rights in, but for that undertaking having one or more nominee shareholders for legal, regulatory or administrative reasons; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>

this Agreement; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

if expressly set out in the body of this Agreement and a reference to this Agreement includes the recitals and Schedules; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
